│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

╭──
│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected
│ ... 59 more lines (ctrl+e to expand)

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

╭──
│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected
│ ... 59 more lines (ctrl+e to expand)

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files

│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

╭──
│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected
│ ... 59 more lines (ctrl+e to expand)

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed

│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:

│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed
│  * message/exchange events for consumption by the enhanced-transcript-monitor.
│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"assistant","content":"I will fix it","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onStepFinish","step":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files
│  * - Tails active files for new content (incremental reads)
│  * - Parses native mastra lifecycle hook format
│  * - Emits 'message' events with role/content/timestamp/metadata
│  * - Emits 'exchange' events when a complete user->assistant turn is detected

│ /**
│  * MastraTranscriptReader - File-watching reader for mastra native transcript format
│  *
│  * Watches mastra lifecycle hook transcript files (NDJSON) and emits parsed

│  *
│  * Mastra lifecycle hooks produce NDJSON files with events like:
│  *   {"type":"session_start","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"message","role":"user","content":"fix the bug","timestamp":"..."}

│  *   {"type":"onToolCall","tool":"...","input":"...","timestamp":"..."}
│  *   {"type":"session_end","sessionId":"abc-123","timestamp":"..."}
│  *
│  * Features:
│  * - Watches a transcript directory for new .jsonl / .ndjson files

This gives network-adaptive routing (VPN → Copilot, outside → Claude subscription).\n- **D-09:** Fix the current mastra observation failure (`GOOGLE_GENERATIVE_AI_API_KEY not found`) by routing observe() through our proxy instead of directly to <COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>.\n\n### Batch Processing & Idempotency\n- **D-10:** Manifest file at `.observations/conversion-manifest.json` tracks which .specstory files have been converted, with content hashes for change detection.\n- **D-11:** `--force` flag to re-process already-converted files.\n- **D-12:** Process files in chronological order (oldest first) to maintain temporal consistency in observations.\n\n### Claude's Discretion\n- Exact MastraDBMessage type shape (determined by @mastra/core's type definitions)\n- Internal chunking strategy for large transcripts (split by exchange or by token count)\n- Progress reporting format during batch conversion (stderr log lines vs progress bar)\n- Whether to use observe() directly or buffer and batch observations\n\n### Folded Todos\n- **LLM-based semantic deduplication** — from pipeline backlog.
